SRONG BTZAN SGAM PO, GNAM RI SRONG BTZAN DANG TSE SPUNG BZA'
GNYIS KYI SRAS, BOD RGYAL GDUNG RABS SO GSUM PA 'DI'I RING LA PO
TA LA'I RI LA PHO BRANG BRTZIGS, BOD YIG GI SROL BTOD, SANGS
RGYAS KYI CHOS THOG MAR BOD YIG TU BSGYUR, BKA' YI KHRIMS YIG
CHEN PO RNAM DRUG MDZAD PA STE, DE YANG DANG PO BOD YUL RU CHEN
LNGA RU PHYE BA DANG, YUL GYI DBANG RIS RNAM PA BCO BRGYAD BCAD
PA, RGOD KYI STONG SDE DRUG CU RTZA GCIG PHYE BA, GA-YUNG GI MI
SDE KHENG DANG YANG KHENG PHYE BA, ZHANG GSUM BLON BCAS DBUS KYI
'DUN SA 'DZIN PA, DPA' SDE GSUM GYIS MTHA' YI SO KHA SRUNG BA
BCAS SRID 'DZIN GNAD DRUG DANG, GNYIS PA BKA' 'GROS CHEN PO DRUG
GSUM PA YIG TSANGS DRUG  BZHI PA BKA' YI PHYAG RGYA DRUG  LNGA
PA RKYEN DRUG  DRUG PA DPA' MTSAN DRUG BCAS DRUG TSAN DRUG GIS
BOD KYI KHOS SUM CU SO DRUG GTAN LA PHAB, LHA CHOS DGE BA BCU
DANG, MI CHOS GTZANG MA BCU DRUG GI SROL BTZUGS NAS RGYAL SRID
BZUNG, BAL BZA' KHRI BTZUN KHAB TU BZHES, LCAGS GLANG LOR RGYA
BZA' WUN SHING KONG JO BTZUN MOR BSUS, RA SA 'PHRUL SNANG GI
GTZUG LAG KHANG DANG, RA MO CHE ZHES PA'I GTZUG LAG KHANG
